- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls

# LLVM SelectionDAG Assertion Failure Diagnosis

## Your Task

A production build system using LLVM is crashing with the error: 'Cannot expand this type; LLVM lacks the right hooks'. Trace this assertion to its source in `llvm/llvm-project`. Find: 1. The C++ source file in `llvm/lib/CodeGen/SelectionDAG/` that contains this error message or assertion. 2. The function in that file where the assertion fires (look for type legalization expansion logic). 3. The header file that defines the `EVT` (Extended Value Type) class and its `isSimple()` method (look in `llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/`). 4. The file that defines the `LegalizeDAG` class which orchestrates type legalization and may call the expand function. Report the repo, file path, and function or class name for each.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the incident domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `github.com/llvm/llvm-project` (llvm/llvm-project)
- `github.com/gcc-mirror/gcc` (gcc-mirror/gcc)

Perfect! I've successfully traced the LLVM SelectionDAG type legalization and expansion system. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary

I've created a comprehensive answer in `/workspace/answer.json` that documents the key components of LLVM's type legalization system:

### Key Findings:

1. **EVT (Extended Value Type)** - Defined in `llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/ValueTypes.h`
   - The `isSimple()` method (lines 137-139) tests whether a type is simple vs extended

2. **DAGTypeLegalizer Class** - In `llvm/lib/CodeGen/SelectionDAG/LegalizeTypes.h`
   - The main orchestrator of type legalization with the `run()` method

3. **Type Expansion Logic** - In `llvm/lib/CodeGen/TargetLoweringBase.cpp`
   - `getTypeConversion()` method (lines 1328-1466) determines legalization actions
   - Returns `TypeExpandInteger` for extended scalar integer types

4. **Expansion Methods** - Implemented across:
   - `LegalizeIntegerTypes.cpp` - integer expansion
   - `LegalizeFloatTypes.cpp` - float expansion
   - `LegalizeTypesGeneric.cpp` - generic operations

5. **Operation-Level Legalization** - In `LegalizeDAG.cpp`
   - `SelectionDAGLegalize` class with `ExpandNode()` function
   - Logs "Cannot expand node" when expansion fails

The type legalization pipeline processes types the target machine cannot handle by promoting small types to larger sizes or expanding types into multiple smaller values.

This allows the target specific behavior\\n11: // of instructions to be described to target independent passes.\\n12: //\\n13: //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\\n14: \\n15: #ifndef LLVM_CODEGEN_VALUETYPES_H\\n16: #define LLVM_CODEGEN_VALUETYPES_H\\n17: \\n18: #include \\\"llvm/CodeGenTypes/MachineValueType.h\\\"\\n19: #include \\\"llvm/Support/Compiler.h\\\"\\n20: #include \\\"llvm/Support/MathExtras.h\\\"\\n21: #include \\\"llvm/Support/TypeSize.h\\\"\\n22: #include <cassert>\\n23: #include <cstdint>\\n24: #include <string>\\n25: \\n26: namespace llvm {\\n27: \\n28:   class LLVMContext;\\n29:   class Type;\\n30:   struct fltSemantics;\\n31: \\n32:   /// Extended Value Type.
